 It is said about any language that if you get to know about the adjectives used in it, then you can speak and write well in that language
 angreji bhashapar bhi yah cheez lagu hoti he
 Although it is easy to get information about Adjectives in English, but some Adjectives can cause problems
 ham aapako udhaaharan ke madhyam se Comparative Adjective or Superlative Adjective ke bare main bataaenge
 See for example
 
 1
 Mohan is smarter than shyamyaham do vyaktiyon kii tulana kii gai he, yahaan Smarter (comparative Degree) he
 It is used to compare two persons
 2
 Mohan is the smartest boy in the Class The term used here is Smartest (superlative Degree)
 iskaa prayog do yaa do se adhik logon yaa vastuon kii tulana karne ke liye kiya jaataa he
 Some Adjectives cannot be made Comparative and Superlative by just applying er and est
 jaaniye kuch aise hi Adjectives ke bare main jo kisi bhi fiks niyam ko follow nahin karte hai

 tippaniyan From his office is seen a crowd of people outside the Reserve Bank of India, who stand to exchange notes

 " goraksha ke naam par bane sanghathanon par pratibandh lagane kii maang vaali yachika par supreme court main sunwaayee hui
 The Supreme Court turned down the demand of the petitioner Tehseen Poonawala, stating that a police officer should be appointed to supervise the cases related to the guards in every district
 yachika main kaha gaya tha ki agar aisi koi ghatana hoti he to us afasar ko jimmedaar tehraaya jaae
 The Supreme Court said that we will not issue any such order
 pehle centre or rajyon ke jawaab aane chahie
 The court has asked the Center and five states to file replies within six weeks
 karnataka apana jawaab daakhil kar chukaa he
 At the same time, the World Gauraksha Vahini has also filed an application in the case, saying that the petition demanding ban on gau rakshaks should be rejected
 court ne use bhi paksh rakhane kii ijaajat di he
 In the last hearing, the Supreme Court issued notice to 6 states and sought answers
 gujarat, rajasthan, jharkhand, maharashtra, uttar pradesh or karnataka ko notice jari kiya tha
 The petitioner stated that Rajasthan did not file an answer in the case
 unhen haalia hui ghatana (alvar vaali) par bhi jawaab dene ko kaha jaae
 However, the court did not say anything on this
 goraksha ke naam par bane sanghathanon par pratibandh lagane kii maang ko lekar daayar janhit yachika par supreme court sunwaayee kar rahaa he
 In the previous hearing, the Supreme Court had sought answers from the Center and the six state governments on the issue, but a notice has been issued for non-filing of replies
 yachikakarta tahseen poonawala ne goraksha ke naam par daliton or alpsankhyakon ke khilaaf ho rahi hinsa rokane kii maang kii he or kaha he ki aisi hinsa karne vaale sanghathanon par usee tarah se pabandi lagaai jaae jis tarah kii pabandi simi jaise sanghathan par lagi he
 It has been said in the petition that in some states in the country, the cow protection parties have received government recognition, due to which their spirits have increased
 maang kii gai he ki gaurakshak dalon kii sarkari manyata samaapt kii jaae
 Along with the petition, videos and newspaper cuttings of violence of the guard parties have been installed and the court has been asked to take cognizance of them
 yachika main kaha gaya he ki gaushala main gaay kii maut or goraksha ke naam par gaurakshak kanoon ko apane haath main le rahe hai
 The petition urges the Uttar Pradesh, Maharashtra, Gujarat, and Karnataka laws to declare the law unconstitutional, which provides for the registration of monitoring groups to protect cows
 yachika main kaha gaya ki goraksha nigaraanee samooh kanoon kedaayre se baahar jaakar kaam kar rahe hai
 The guardians are torturing the name of cow protection and the crimes committed by them are not only within the purview of the Indian Penal Code but also under the purview of the SC / ST Act, 1989
 yachika main 'salwa judum (naksal virdohi samooh) maamle main supreme court dwaara varsh 2011 main die us faisle kaa hawala diya gaya he jisamen salwa judum par pabandi lagaai gai thi
 The comments yachika main kaha gaya ki kanoon ke tahat mili sangrakshan kii vajah se aise log hinsa bhadakaane kaa kaam karte hai or alpsankhyakon or daliton par atyaachaar karte hai
 It may be known that the provisions of the Gujarat Animal Prevention Act, 1956 stated that people exercising their rights under this Act would be considered as government jobs
 maharashtra or karnataka main bhi isi tarah ke praavdhaan hai
 The petition, while referring to the incident of beating of Dalits in Una and East Godavari district, said that such groups are a threat to the rule of law
 saath hi yah mare hue jaanwaron kaa khaal utaarne ke peshey main lage logon ke mul adhikaron ke khilaaf he
 The petition said that the officer should be held responsible if any such incident occurs
 supreme court ne kaha ki ham aisa koi aadesh jari nahin karenge
 The answers of the Center and the States should come first
 court ne centre or paanch rajyon ko chah hafte main jawaab daakhil karne ko kaha he
 Karnataka has filed its reply
 vahiin vishwa gausuraksha vahini ne bhi maamle main arji daakhil kar kaha he ki gaurakshakon par pratibandh lagane kii maang vaali yachika ko khaarij kar dena chahie
 The court has also allowed him to stand
 pichhali sunwaayee main supreme court ne 6 rajyon ko notice jari kar jawaab maanga tha
 Notices were issued to Gujarat, Rajasthan, Jharkhand, Maharashtra, Uttar Pradesh and Karnataka
 yachikakarta ne kaha ki rajasthan ne is maamle main jawaab daakhil nahin kiya
 They may also be asked to respond to the recent incident (alwar Wali)
 haalanki court ne is par kuch nahin kaha
 The Supreme Court is hearing a public interest litigation seeking a ban on organizations named in the name of cow protection
 pichhali sunwaayee main is mudde par supreme court ne centre or chah rajya sarkaron se jawaab maanga tha lekin jawaab daakhil na karne par notice jari kiya gaya he
 Petitioner Tehsin Poonawala has sought to stop the violence against Dalits and minorities in the name of cow protection and has said that such violence organizations should be banned in the same manner as the organization like SIMI
 yachika main kaha gaya he ki desh main kuch rajyon main goraksha dalon ko sarkari manyata mili hui he jisase inke haunsale bade hue hai
 There has been a demand that government recognition of guard teams be abolished
 yachika ke saath main gaurakshak dalon kii hinsa ke video or akhbaar kii kating lagaai gai hai or adaalat se inkaa sangyaan lene ko kaha gaya he
 The petition said that in the name of cow's death and cow protection in the cowshed, the gaurakshak is taking the law into its own hands
 yachika main uttar pradesh, maharashtra, gujarat, or karnataka ke us kanoon ko asanvaidhanik qaraar dene kii guhaar kii gai he, jisamen gaay kii raksha ke liye nigaraanee samoohon ke panjikaran kaa praavdhaan he
 The petition said that the cow protection watchdog groups are working outside the jurisdiction of the law
 goraksha kenam par gaurakshak atyaachaar kar rahe hai or unkedvara kiye jane vaale aparaadh na keval bhartiya dand samhita ke daayre main hai balki essi / asti act, 1989 ke daayre main bhi he
 The petition cited the Supreme Court judgment in 2011 in the Salwa Judum (anti-naxalite group) case in which Salwa Judum was banned
 tippaniyan The petition said that due to the protection provided under the law, such people act to incite violence and persecute minorities and Dalits
 maaloom ho ki gujarat pashu rokthaam adhinium, 1956 ke praavdhaanon main kaha gaya ki is adhinium ke tahat apane adhikaron kaa istemaal karne vaale log sarkari naukari maane jaaenge
 Maharashtra and Karnataka also have similar provisions
 yachika main oona or purvi godavari jile main daliton kii pitayee kii ghatana kaa zikr karte hue kaha gaya he ki aise samooh kanoon ke shashan ke liye khatra hai
 At the same time it is against the basic rights of people engaged in the profession of skinning dead animals

 soochnaaon ke badale miltaa tha paisaarope he ki keke ranjit ne yuavi or vayusena ke vimaanon ke bare main kai ahm jaankaree pahunchaai
 He also provided all confidential photographs
 iske evaj main khufia agency ne uske khate main paise bhi dalwaae
 He was posted in Delhi from 2010 to 2013
 usne 26 janvari 2011 kii parade main bhi hissaa liya tha
